````
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/README.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: # MIMO Platform
2: 
3: A minimal, Emacs-style web-based editor for AI-assisted development.
4: 
5: ## Overview
6: 
7: MIMO (Minimal IDE for Modern Operations) is a platform that enables AI-assisted development through a web-based interface with an Emacs-style workflow. It provides session-based development with worktrees, file synchronization, and integrated chat with AI agents.
8: 
9: ## Features
10: 
11: - **Emacs-Style Interface**: Three-buffer layout with customizable keybindings
12: - **Session-Based Development**: Work with isolated worktrees for each development session
13: - **File Synchronization**: Automatic sync between agent worktree and original repository
14: - **Integrated Chat**: Real-time chat with AI agents via WebSocket
15: - **VCS Integration**: Fossil as intermediary for both Git and Fossil repositories
16: - **Agent Lifecycle**: Spawn and manage AI agents with JWT authentication
17: - **Conflict Detection**: Smart conflict detection with baseline checksums
18: 
19: ## Architecture
20: 
21: ```
22: ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
23: │                      Browser (Client)                       │
24: │  ┌─────────────┐  ┌─────────────┐  ┌─────────────────┐   │
25: │  │ Files Tree  │  │   Chat      │  │    Changes      │   │
26: │  │   (Left)    │  │  (Center)   │  │    (Right)      │   │
27: │  └─────────────┘  └─────────────┘  └─────────────────┘   │
28: └─────────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────┘
29:                           │ WebSocket / HTTP
30: ┌─────────────────────────▼─────────────────────────────────┐
31: │                 mimo-platform (Hono/Bun)                   │
32: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
33: │  │  Auth  │  Projects  │  Sessions  │  Agents  │ Sync │  │
34: │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
35: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
36: │  │              WebSocket Handlers                      │  │
37: │  │         (Chat, Agent Connections)                  │  │
38: │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
39: └─────────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────┘
40:                           │
41: ┌─────────────────────────▼─────────────────────────────────┐
42: │                   mimo-agent (Binary)                      │
43: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
44: │  │         File Watcher  │  ACP Process Proxy        │  │
45: │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
46: └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
47: ```
48: 
49: ## Installation
50: 
51: ### Prerequisites
52: 
53: - [Bun](https://bun.sh) 1.0+
54: - [Fossil](https://fossil-scm.org) 2.27+
55: - Git (for Git repository support)
56: 
57: ### Quick Start
58: 
59: ```bash
60: # Clone the repository
61: git clone https://github.com/your-org/mimo.git
62: cd mimo
63: 
64: # Install dependencies
65: cd packages/mimo-platform
66: bun install
67: 
68: # Start the server
69: bun run dev
70: ```
71: 
72: The platform will be available at `http://localhost:3000`
73: 
74: ### Build the Agent
75: 
76: ```bash
77: cd packages/mimo-agent
78: bun install
79: bun run build
80: ```
81: 
82: This creates `dist/mimo-agent` which is used by the platform.
83: 
84: ## Usage
85: 
86: ### Authentication
87: 
88: 1. Navigate to `http://localhost:3000/auth/register`
89: 2. Create an account
90: 3. Login at `http://localhost:3000/auth/login`
91: 
92: ### Creating a Project
93: 
94: 1. Click "New Project" on the projects page
95: 2. Enter project name
96: 3. Provide Git or Fossil repository URL
97: 4. The system imports/clones the repository
98: 
99: ### Starting a Session
100: 
101: 1. Select a project from the projects list
102: 2. Click "New Session"
103: 3. Enter session name
104: 4. The system sets up a Fossil worktree
105: 
106: ### Working with Agents
107: 
108: 1. In a session, click "Start Agent"
109: 2. The platform spawns an agent process
110: 3. Chat with the agent in the center buffer
111: 4. File changes appear in the right buffer automatically
112: 
113: ### Committing Changes
114: 
115: 1. Make changes through the agent
116: 2. Click "Commit" button or press `C-x c`
117: 3. Enter commit message
118: 4. Changes are committed to Fossil and pushed to the original repository
119: 
120: ## Configuration
121: 
122: Configuration is stored in `~/.mimo/config.yaml`:
123: 
124: ```yaml
125: theme: dark
126: fontSize: 14
127: fontFamily: monospace
128: keybindings:
129:   cancel_request: "C-c C-c"
130:   commit: "C-x c"
131:   find_file: "C-x C-f"
132:   switch_project: "C-x p"
133:   switch_session: "C-x s"
134:   focus_left: "C-x h"
135:   focus_center: "C-x j"
136:   focus_right: "C-x l"
137: ```
138: 
139: Edit via the web UI at `/config` or directly in the file.
140: 
141: ## Directory Structure
142: 
143: ```
144: ~/.mimo/
145: ├── config.yaml           # User configuration
146: ├── users/
147: │   └── {username}/
148: │       └── credentials.yaml
149: ├── projects/
150: │   └── {project-id}/
151: │       ├── project.yaml
152: │       ├── repo.fossil
153: │       ├── original/     # Original repo worktree
154: │       └── sessions/
155: │           └── {session-id}/
156: │               ├── session.yaml
157: │               └── chat.jsonl
158: └── agents/
159:     └── {agent-id}/
160:         └── agent.yaml
161: ```
162: 
163: ## Development
164: 
165: ```bash
166: # Run tests
167: bun test
168: 
169: # Run with hot reload
170: bun run dev
171: 
172: # Build for production
173: bun run build
174: ```
175: 
176: ## License
177: 
178: MIT License - see LICENSE file for details.
179: 
180: ## Contributing
181: 
182: Contributions are welcome! Please read CONTRIBUTING.md for guidelines.

(End of file - total 182 lines)
</content>
````

import { Hono } from "hono";

let projectRepository: any;
let userRepository: any;

describe("Public Landing Page Integration Tests", () => {
  const testHome = join(tmpdir(), `mimo-landing-test-${Date.now()}`);

  beforeEach(async () => {
    process.env.MIMO_HOME = testHome;
    process.env.JWT_SECRET = "test-secret-key-for-testing";

    try {
      rmSync(testHome, { recursive: true, force: true });
    } catch {}

    const pathsModule = await import("../src/config/paths.ts");
    pathsModule.ensureMimoHome();

    const userModule = await import("../src/auth/user.ts");
    userRepository = userModule.userRepository;

    const projectModule = await import("../src/projects/repository.ts");
    projectRepository = projectModule.projectRepository;

    app = new Hono();
    
    const authModule = await import("../src/auth/routes.tsx");
    app.route("/auth", authModule.default);

    const protectedModule = await import("../src/protected/routes.tsx");
    app.route("/", protectedModule.default);

    const projectsModule = await import("../src/projects/routes.tsx");
    app.route("/projects", projectsModule.default);

    const LandingPageModule = await import("../src/components/LandingPage.tsx");
    const LandingPage = LandingPageModule.LandingPage;

    app.get("/", async (c) => {
      const publicProjects = await projectRepository.listAllPublic();
      const user = c.get("user") as { username: string } | undefined;
      const isAuthenticated = !!user;
      const username = user?.username;
      return c.html(<LandingPage projects={publicProjects} isAuthenticated={isAuthenticated} username={username} />);
    });

    app.get("/api/projects/public", async (c) => {
      const publicProjects = await projectRepository.listAllPublic();
      return c.json(publicProjects);
    });
  });

- **Public Landing Page**: View platform overview and public projects without authentication
- **Project Descriptions**: Add optional descriptions to projects for better discoverability
- **Emacs-Style Interface**: Three-buffer layout with customizable keybindings
- **Session-Based Development**: Work with isolated worktrees for each development session
- **File Synchronization**: Automatic sync between agent worktree and original repository
- **Integrated Chat**: Real-time chat with AI agents via WebSocket
- **VCS Integration**: Fossil as intermediary for both Git and Fossil repositories
- **Agent Lifecycle**: Spawn and manage AI agents with JWT authentication
- **Conflict Detection**: Smart conflict detection with baseline checksums

newString: ## Usage

### Public Landing Page

When you first navigate to `http://localhost:3000`, you'll see a public landing page displaying:
- Platform overview and features
- List of all public projects (names, descriptions, owners, repo types)
- Login and Register buttons

Clicking on a project card will redirect you to login if not authenticated, or take you directly to the project detail if authenticated.

### Authentication

1. Navigate to `http://localhost:3000/auth/register`
2. Create an account
3. Login at `http://localhost:3000/auth/login`

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/mimo-platform/specs/session-management/spec.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:06:58
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/mimo-platform/specs/session-management/spec.md

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/mimo-platform/specs/session-management/spec.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## ADDED Requirements
2: 
3: ### Requirement: User can create a session
4: The system SHALL allow users to create sessions within a project. Each session creates a worktree and starts a Fossil server.
5: 
6: #### Scenario: Create session with title
7: - **WHEN** authenticated user submits session title "fix-auth-bug" for project "my-app"
8: - **THEN** system creates directory ~/.mimo/projects/my-app/sessions/fix-auth-bug/
9: - **AND** system clones project's repository to repo.fossil
10: - **AND** system assigns auto-generated port (8000-9000 range)
11: - **AND** system starts Fossil server on assigned port
12: - **AND** system stores session.yaml with {title: "fix-auth-bug", port: <assigned>, status: "active"}
13: - **AND** system displays session view
14: 
15: #### Scenario: Port collision handling
16: - **WHEN** system attempts to start Fossil server on occupied port
17: - **THEN** system tries next available port in range
18: - **AND** system continues until successful
19: 
20: #### Scenario: Duplicate session title
21: - **WHEN** user submits session title that already exists in project
22: - **THEN** system appends timestamp to title or returns error
23: 
24: ### Requirement: Session persists across disconnects
25: The system SHALL maintain session state when user disconnects.
26: 
27: #### Scenario: Reconnect to active session
28: - **WHEN** user reconnects to existing session
29: - **THEN** system loads chat history from messages.jsonl
30: - **AND** system reattaches to running agent if exists
31: - **AND** system displays current file tree state
32: 
33: #### Scenario: Agent running on reconnect
34: - **WHEN** user reconnects and agent is still running
35: - **THEN** system establishes WebSocket to agent
36: - **AND** system resumes chat stream
37: 
38: ### Requirement: User can delete a session
39: The system SHALL allow users to remove sessions.
40: 
41: #### Scenario: Delete session with cleanup
42: - **WHEN** authenticated user deletes session "fix-auth-bug"
43: - **THEN** system terminates agent process if running
44: - **AND** system stops Fossil server
45: - **AND** system removes ~/.mimo/projects/my-app/sessions/fix-auth-bug/ directory
46: 
47: ### Requirement: Chat messages are stored persistently
48: The system SHALL store chat history in append-only JSONL format.
49: 
50: #### Scenario: Store user message
51: - **WHEN** user sends message "Add dark mode"
52: - **THEN** system appends to messages.jsonl: {type: "user", content: "Add dark mode", timestamp: "..."}
53: 
54: #### Scenario: Store agent message
55: - **WHEN** agent sends response "I'll help with that..."
56: - **THEN** system appends to messages.jsonl: {type: "agent", content: "...", timestamp: "..."}
57: 
58: #### Scenario: Stream agent response
59: - **WHEN** agent streams response in chunks
60: - **THEN** system buffers and stores complete message on finish
61: - **AND** system displays streaming updates via WebSocket
62: 
63: ### Requirement: Session shows file tree with change indicators
64: The system SHALL display project file tree with modification markers in the left buffer.
65: 
66: #### Scenario: Show modified files
67: - **WHEN** agent reports file changes
68: - **THEN** system marks files with [M] in file tree (left buffer)
69: - **AND** system updates changes buffer (right buffer)
70: 
71: #### Scenario: Show new files
72: - **WHEN** agent creates new files
73: - **THEN** system marks files with [?] in file tree (left buffer)
74: 
75: ### Requirement: Session shows file diffs with syntax highlighting
76: The system SHALL display file changes with language-appropriate syntax highlighting.
77: 
78: #### Scenario: View file diff
79: - **WHEN** user clicks on modified file
80: - **THEN** system displays diff with syntax highlighting
81: - **AND** system shows line additions and deletions
82: 
83: ### Requirement: User can navigate file tree
84: The system SHALL allow users to browse and open files.
85: 
86: #### Scenario: Find file
87: - **WHEN** user presses the configured keybinding for find_file
88: - **THEN** system prompts for file path
89: - **AND** system opens file in file buffer
90: 
91: #### Scenario: Click file in tree
92: - **WHEN** user clicks file in file tree
93: - **THEN** system loads file content into file buffer
94: 
95: ### Requirement: Keybindings are configurable
96: The system SHALL allow users to customize keybindings stored in ~/.mimo/config.yaml.
97: 
98: #### Scenario: Load custom keybindings
99: - **WHEN** user starts platform
100: - **THEN** system reads ~/.mimo/config.yaml
101: - **AND** system loads custom keybindings if defined
102: - **AND** system uses defaults for missing bindings
103: 
104: #### Scenario: Use default keybinding
105: - **WHEN** user presses C-c C-c (default cancel)
106: - **THEN** system executes cancel agent command
107: - **AND** keybinding is configurable via config.yaml
108: 
109: #### Scenario: Focus buffer with keybinding
110: - **WHEN** user presses C-x h
111: - **THEN** system focuses file buffer (left)
112: - **AND** system updates active buffer indicator
113: 
114: #### Scenario: Focus chat buffer
115: - **WHEN** user presses C-x j
116: - **THEN** system focuses chat buffer (center)
117: - **AND** system updates active buffer indicator
118: 
119: #### Scenario: Focus changes buffer
120: - **WHEN** user presses C-x l
121: - **THEN** system focuses changes buffer (right)
122: - **AND** system updates active buffer indicator

(End of file - total 122 lines)
</content>
```

<content>1: /** @jsx jsx */
2: import { jsx } from "hono/jsx";
3: import { Hono } from "hono";
4: import { getCookie } from "hono/cookie";
5: import { sessionRepository } from "./repository.js";
6: import { projectRepository } from "../projects/repository.js";
7: import { agentService } from "../agents/service.js";
8: import { chatService } from "./chat.js";
9: import { vcs } from "../vcs/index.js";
10: import { verifyToken } from "../auth/jwt.js";
11: import { Layout } from "../components/Layout.js";
12: import { SessionDetailPage } from "../components/SessionDetailPage.js";

14: import { SessionListPage } from "../components/SessionListPage.js";
15: import type { Context } from "hono";
16: 
17: const router = new Hono();
18: 
19: // Helper to get authenticated username from cookie
20: async function getAuthUsername(c: Context): Promise<string | null> {
21:   const cookieHeader = c.req.header("Cookie");
22:   const usernameMatch = cookieHeader?.match(/username=([^;]+)/);
23:   const username = usernameMatch ? usernameMatch[1] : null;
24:   if (username) return username;
25:   
26:   // Also check JWT token
27:   const tokenMatch = cookieHeader?.match(/token=([^;]+)/);
28:   const token = tokenMatch ? tokenMatch[1] : null;
29:   
30:   if (token) {
31:     const payload = await verifyToken(token);
32:     if (payload) return payload.username;
33:   }
34:   
35:   return null;
36: }
37: 
38: // Helper to get projectId from either URL param or query param
39: function getProjectId(c: Context): string | null {
40:   // Try URL param first (for nested routes)
41:   const projectId = c.req.param("projectId");
42:   if (projectId) return projectId;
43:   
44:   // Fall back to query param (for flat routes)
45:   return c.req.query("projectId");
46: }
47: 
48: // GET /sessions or /projects/:projectId/sessions - List sessions for a project
49: router.get("/", async (c: Context) => {
50:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
51:   if (!username) {
52:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
53:   }
54: 
55:   const projectId = getProjectId(c);
56:   if (!projectId) {
57:     return c.text("Project ID required", 400);
58:   }
59: 
60:   const project = await projectRepository.findById(projectId);
61:   if (!project || project.owner !== username) {
62:     return c.text("Project not found", 404);
63:   }
64: 
65:   const sessions = await sessionRepository.listByProject(projectId);
66:   
67:   return c.html(
68:     <Layout title={`Sessions - ${project.name}`}>
69:       <SessionListPage project={project} sessions={sessions} />
70:     </Layout>
71:   );
72: });
73: 
74: // GET /sessions/new or /projects/:projectId/sessions/new - Create session form
75: router.get("/new", async (c: Context) => {
76:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
77:   if (!username) {
78:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
79:   }
80: 
81:   const projectId = getProjectId(c);
82:   if (!projectId) {
83:     return c.text("Project ID required", 400);

98: // POST /sessions or /projects/:projectId/sessions - Create new session
99: router.post("/", async (c: Context) => {
100:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
101:   if (!username) {
102:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
103:   }
104: 
105:   const body = await c.req.parseBody();
106:   const name = body.name as string;
107:   const projectId = (body.projectId as string) || getProjectId(c);
108: 
109:   if (!name || !projectId) {
110:     return c.text("Name and project ID required", 400);
111:   }
112: 
113:   const project = await projectRepository.findById(projectId);
114:   if (!project || project.owner !== username) {
115:     return c.text("Project not found", 404);
116:   }
117: 
118:   // Create session with worktree
119:   const session = await sessionRepository.create({
120:     name: name as string,
121:     projectId: projectId as string,
122:     owner: username,
123:     worktreePath: "", // Will be set by repository
124:   });
125: 
126:   // Initialize worktree from Fossil repository
127:   try {
128:     await vcs.setupSessionWorktree(projectId, session.id, session.worktreePath);
129:   } catch (error) {
130:     console.error("Failed to setup worktree:", error);
131:     // Don't fail - user can still see the session
132:   }
133: 
134:   return c.redirect(`/projects/${projectId}/sessions/${session.id}`);
135: });
136: 
137: // GET /sessions/:id or /projects/:projectId/sessions/:id - View session detail
138: router.get("/:id", async (c: Context) => {
139:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
140:   if (!username) {
141:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
142:   }
143: 
144:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
145:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
146:   
147:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
148:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
149:   }
150: 
151:   const project = await projectRepository.findById(session.projectId);
152:   if (!project) {
153:     return c.text("Project not found", 404);
154:   }
155: 
156:   // Get chat history
157:   const chatHistory = await chatService.loadHistory(sessionId);
158:   
159:   // Get agent status
160:   const agents = await agentService.listAgentsBySession(sessionId);
161:   const activeAgent = agents.find(a => a.status === "connected");
162: 
163:   // Get file changes
164:   const { fileSyncService } = await import("../sync/service.js");
165:   const changeSet = await fileSyncService.getChangeSet(sessionId);
166:   const hasConflicts = changeSet.hasConflicts;
167: 
168:   return c.html(
169:     <Layout title={session.name}>
170:       <SessionDetailPage 
171:         session={session}
172:         project={project}
173:         chatHistory={chatHistory}
174:         activeAgent={activeAgent}
175:         changes={changeSet.files}
176:         hasConflicts={hasConflicts}
177:       />
178:     </Layout>
179:   );
180: });
181: 
182: // POST /sessions/:id/agent or /projects/:projectId/sessions/:id/agent - Spawn an agent
183: router.post("/:id/agent", async (c: Context) => {
184:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
185:   if (!username) {
186:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
187:   }
188: 
189:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
190:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
191:   
192:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
193:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
194:   }
195: 
196:   // Check if there's already an active agent
197:   const existingAgents = await agentService.listAgentsBySession(sessionId);
198:   const activeAgent = existingAgents.find(a => a.status === "connected" || a.status === "starting");
199:   
200:   if (activeAgent) {
201:     return c.redirect(`/sessions/${sessionId}`);
202:   }
203: 
204:   try {
205:     await agentService.spawnAgent({
206:       sessionId,
207:       projectId: session.projectId,
208:       owner: username,
209:     });
210:   } catch (error) {
211:     console.error("Failed to spawn agent:", error);
212:     // Error is handled by service - it updates status and adds chat message
213:   }
214: 
215:   return c.redirect(`/projects/${session.projectId}/sessions/${sessionId}`);
216: });
217: 
218: // POST /sessions/:id/cancel - Cancel current ACP request
219: router.post("/:id/cancel", async (c: Context) => {
220:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
221:   if (!username) {
222:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
223:   }
224: 
225:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
226:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
227:   
228:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
229:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
230:   }
231: 
232:   const cancelled = await agentService.cancelCurrentRequest(sessionId);
233:   
234:   return c.json({ success: cancelled });
235: });
236: 
237: // POST /sessions/:id/delete or /projects/:projectId/sessions/:id/delete - Delete session
238: router.post("/:id/delete", async (c: Context) => {
239:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
240:   if (!username) {
241:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
242:   }
243: 
244:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
245:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
246:   
247:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
248:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
249:   }
250: 
251:   // Kill any active agents
252:   await agentService.killAgentsBySession(sessionId);
253: 
254:   // Delete session
255:   await sessionRepository.delete(session.projectId, sessionId);
256: 
257:   return c.redirect(`/projects/${session.projectId}/sessions`);
258: });
259: 
260: // GET /sessions/:id/files - Get file tree for a session
261: router.get("/:id/files", async (c: Context) => {
262:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
263:   if (!username) {
264:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
265:   }
266: 
267:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
268:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
269:   
270:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
271:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
272:   }
273: 
274:   // Scan filesystem directly for files
275:   const { readdirSync, statSync } = await import("fs");
276:   const { join, relative } = await import("path");
277:   
278:   const fileTree: { [key: string]: string[] } = {};
279:   
280:   function scanDir(dirPath: string, basePath: string) {
281:     if (!statSync(dirPath, { throwIfNoEntry: false })) {
282:       return;
283:     }
284:     
285:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
286:     
287:     for (const entry of entries) {
288:       const fullPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
289:       const relPath = relative(basePath, fullPath);
290:       
291:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
292:         scanDir(fullPath, basePath);
293:       } else {
294:         const parts = relPath.split("/");
295:         const fileName = parts.pop() || "";
296:         const dir = parts.length > 0 ? parts.join("/") : "(root)";
297:         
298:         if (!fileTree[dir]) {
299:           fileTree[dir] = [];
300:         }
301:         fileTree[dir].push(fileName);
302:       }
303:     }
304:   }
305:   
306:   try {
307:     scanDir(session.worktreePath, session.worktreePath);
308:   } catch (error) {
309:     console.error("Error scanning worktree:", error);
310:   }
311: 
312:   // Return HTML file tree
313:   let html = `<!DOCTYPE html>
314: <html>
315: <head><title>File Tree</title></head>
316: <body>
317: <div class="file-tree">
318: `;
319: 
320:   for (const [dir, files] of Object.entries(fileTree)) {
321:     html += `  <div class="dir">${dir}/</div>\n`;
322:     for (const file of files) {
323:       html += `    <div class="file">${file}</div>\n`;
324:     }
325:   }
326: 
327:   html += `</div>
328: </body>
329: </html>`;
330: 
331:   return c.html(html);
332: });
333: 
334: // POST /sessions/:id/chat - Save a chat message
335: router.post("/:id/chat", async (c: Context) => {
336:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
337:   if (!username) {
338:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
339:   }
340: 
341:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
342:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
343: 
344:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
345:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
346:   }
347: 
348:   const body = await c.req.parseBody();
349:   const message = body.message as string;
350: 
351:   if (!message) {
352:     return c.text("Message required", 400);
353:   }
354: 
355:   await chatService.saveMessage(sessionId, {
356:     role: "user",
357:     content: message,
358:     timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
359:   });
360: 
361:   return c.json({ success: true });
362: });
363: 
364: export default router;

(End of file - total 364 lines)

<content>1: ## ADDED Requirements
2: 
3: ### Requirement: User can create a project
4: The system SHALL allow authenticated users to create projects that can be linked to Git or Fossil repositories.
5: 
6: #### Scenario: Create project with Git repository
7: - **WHEN** authenticated user submits project name "my-app" and Git URL "https://github.com/user/repo.git"
8: - **THEN** system creates directory ~/.mimo/projects/my-app/
9: - **AND** system stores project.yaml with {name: "my-app", repos: [{type: "git", url: "..."}]}
10: - **AND** system redirects to session creation
11: 
12: #### Scenario: Create project with Fossil repository
13: - **WHEN** authenticated user submits project name "my-app" and Fossil URL "https://fossil.example.com/repo"
14: - **THEN** system creates directory ~/.mimo/projects/my-app/
15: - **AND** system stores project.yaml with {name: "my-app", repos: [{type: "fossil", url: "..."}]}
16: 
17: #### Scenario: Create project with multiple repositories
18: - **WHEN** authenticated user submits project name "my-app" with two repository URLs
19: - **THEN** system stores both repositories in project.yaml repos array
20: 
21: #### Scenario: Duplicate project name
22: - **WHEN** user submits project name that already exists
23: - **THEN** system returns error "Project name already exists"
24: 
25: ### Requirement: User can list projects
26: The system SHALL display all projects owned by the authenticated user.
27: 
28: #### Scenario: List user projects
29: - **WHEN** authenticated user navigates to projects page
30: - **THEN** system displays list of all projects from ~/.mimo/projects/
31: - **AND** each project shows name and repository count
32: 
33: #### Scenario: Empty project list
34: - **WHEN** authenticated user with no projects navigates to projects page
35: - **THEN** system displays message "No projects yet. Create one?"
36: 
37: ### Requirement: User can switch between projects
38: The system SHALL allow users to select a project and view its sessions.
39: 
40: #### Scenario: Switch to project
41: - **WHEN** user selects project from list
42: - **THEN** system loads project context
43: - **AND** system displays project's sessions
44: 
45: ### Requirement: User can delete a project
46: The system SHALL allow users to remove projects and all associated sessions.
47: 
48: #### Scenario: Delete project with confirmation
49: - **WHEN** authenticated user confirms deletion of project "my-app"
50: - **THEN** system removes ~/.mimo/projects/my-app/ directory recursively
51: - **AND** system terminates any running agents for project's sessions
52: - **AND** system redirects to projects list

"### Requirement: User can switch between projects

- **THEN** system loads project context

- **AND** system stores project.yaml with {name: "my-app", repos: [{type: "git", url: "..."}]}

<skill_content name="openspec-new-change">
# Skill: openspec-new-change

Start a new change using the experimental artifact-driven approach.

**Input**: The user's request should include a change name (kebab-case) OR a description of what they want to build.

**Steps**

1. **If no clear input provided, ask what they want to build**

   Use the **AskUserQuestion tool** (open-ended, no preset options) to ask:
   > "What change do you want to work on? Describe what you want to build or fix."

   From their description, derive a kebab-case name (e.g., "add user authentication" → `add-user-auth`).

   **IMPORTANT**: Do NOT proceed without understanding what the user wants to build.

2. **Determine the workflow schema**

   Use the default schema (omit `--schema`) unless the user explicitly requests a different workflow.

   **Use a different schema only if the user mentions:**
   - A specific schema name → use `--schema <name>`
   - "show workflows" or "what workflows" → run `openspec schemas --json` and let them choose

   **Otherwise**: Omit `--schema` to use the default.

3. **Create the change directory**
   ```bash
   openspec new change "<name>"
   ```
   Add `--schema <name>` only if the user requested a specific workflow.
   This creates a scaffolded change at `openspec/changes/<name>/` with the selected schema.

4. **Show the artifact status**
   ```bash
   openspec status --change "<name>"
   ```
   This shows which artifacts need to be created and which are ready (dependencies satisfied).

5. **Get instructions for the first artifact**
   The first artifact depends on the schema (e.g., `proposal` for spec-driven).
   Check the status output to find the first artifact with status "ready".
   ```bash
   openspec instructions <first-artifact-id> --change "<name>"
   ```
   This outputs the template and context for creating the first artifact.

6. **STOP and wait for user direction**

**Output**

After completing the steps, summarize:
- Change name and location
- Schema/workflow being used and its artifact sequence
- Current status (0/N artifacts complete)
- The template for the first artifact
- Prompt: "Ready to create the first artifact? Just describe what this change is about and I'll draft it, or ask me to continue."

**Guardrails**
- Do NOT create any artifacts yet - just show the instructions
- Do NOT advance beyond showing the first artifact template
- If the name is invalid (not kebab-case), ask for a valid name
- If a change with that name already exists, suggest continuing that change instead
- Pass --schema if using a non-default workflow

Base directory for this skill: file:///home/bit4bit/src/mimo/.opencode/skills/openspec-new-change
Relative paths in this skill (e.g., scripts/, reference/) are relative to this base directory.
Note: file list is sampled.

<skill_files>

</skill_files>
</skill_content>
````

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/project-sessions-link/proposal.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:09:27
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/project-sessions-link/proposal.md
content: ## Why

Users cannot view or create sessions from the project detail page. When viewing a project, users see project metadata but have no visibility into existing sessions or a way to start new development sessions. The project-management spec states that selecting a project should "display project's sessions," but this requirement is not implemented.

## What Changes

- **NEW**: Sessions section on ProjectDetailPage showing list of existing sessions
- **NEW**: "New Session" button linking to `/projects/:id/sessions/new`
- **NEW**: Session list with session name, status, and link to session detail
- **MODIFIED**: ProjectDetailPage to include sessions UI alongside project metadata

## Capabilities

### New Capabilities

- `project-session-overview`: Users can view all sessions for a project and create new sessions directly from the project detail page

### Modified Capabilities

- `project-management`: Add requirement for displaying sessions on project detail page (already partially specified but not implemented)

## Impact

**Files Modified:**
- `src/components/ProjectDetailPage.tsx` - Add session list section and "New Session" button

**Dependencies:**
- Existing session routes (`/projects/:projectId/sessions`)
- Existing session repository (`listByProject`)
- Existing ProjectDetailPage component

**No Breaking Changes:** This is purely additive - adds UI elements to an existing page.

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-04 00:09:33)

The change is about adding sessions visibility to the project detail page.
## Agent (2026-04-04 00:09:33)

I'll create the design document for the project-sessions-link change.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/project-sessions-link/design.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:09:50
**Parameters:**
content: ## Context

The MIMO platform currently has a ProjectDetailPage that shows project metadata (name, description, repo URL, type, owner, created date) but provides no visibility into sessions. Users must manually navigate to `/projects/:projectId/sessions` to view or create sessions, which is not discoverable.

The session management functionality already exists:
- `GET /projects/:projectId/sessions` - Lists sessions for a project
- `GET /projects/:projectId/sessions/new` - Shows session creation form
- `POST /projects/:projectId/sessions` - Creates a new session
- SessionRepository has `listByProject(projectId)` method

## Goals / Non-Goals

**Goals:**
- Display existing sessions on the ProjectDetailPage
- Provide a clear "New Session" button to start development
- Show session name, ID, and status for each session
- Link sessions to their detail pages

**Non-Goals:**
- Session creation directly on project page (keep separate form)
- Session filtering or search (future enhancement)
- Session statistics or metrics (future enhancement)
- Deleting sessions from project page (keep on session detail)

## Decisions

### 1. Session Section Placement

**Decision:** Add a "Sessions" section below project details and above the actions section.

**Rationale:**
- Sessions are the primary workflow in MIMO - users create sessions to work on code
- Placing after project details provides context before actions
- Natural reading flow: project info → sessions → actions

**Alternatives considered:**
- Tab-based UI: Over-engineered for current needs, can add later if needed
- Side-by-side layout: Doesn't work well on mobile/tablet, more complex
- Separate sessions page: Existing, but lack of discoverability is the problem

### 2. Session List Display

**Decision:** Show session name, creation date, and link to session detail.

**Rationale:**
- Minimal but useful information
- Consistent with existing project list pattern
- Clicking session name navigates to session detail page

**Implementation:**
```tsx
<div class="sessions-section">
  <h2>Sessions</h2>
  {sessions.length === 0 ? (
    <p>No sessions yet. Create one to start development.</p>
  ) : (
    <ul>
      {sessions.map(session => (
        <li>
          <a href={`/projects/${projectId}/sessions/${session.id}`}>{session.name}</a>
          <span>{new Date(session.createdAt).toLocaleDateString()}</span>
        </li>
      ))}
    </ul>
  )}
  <a href={`/projects/${projectId}/sessions/new`} class="btn">New Session</a>
</div>
```

### 3. Data Fetching

**Decision:** Fetch sessions server-side in the existing `/projects/:id` route handler.

**Rationale:**
- Consistent with existing patterns (project list fetches projects)
- No additional API calls from client
- Simple to implement - just add one repository call

**Implementation:**
```typescript
// In routes.tsx, GET /projects/:id
const sessions = await sessionRepository.listByProject(project.id);
return c.html(<ProjectDetailPage project={project} sessions={sessions} />);
```

## Risks / Trade-offs

**Risk:** Many sessions could make page long
→ **Mitigation:** Show most recent 5 sessions with "View All" link (future), or add pagination

**Risk:** Stale session data if sessions change frequently
→ **Mitigation:** Not a concern - page loads fresh on each request, no caching

**Risk:** Performance impact from additional database call
→ **Mitigation:** Session list is small (typically <10), minimal overhead

**Trade-off:** No real-time session status updates
→ **Future:** Could add WebSocket for live status, but not needed for MVP

## Migration Plan

1. Deploy code changes (no data migration needed)
2. Users immediately see sessions on project detail page
3. No rollback needed - additive change

## Open Questions

1. **Should we show active agents count per session?**
   - **Decision:** No, keep minimal. Can add later if needed.

2. **Should "New Session" be primary (filled) or secondary (outline) button?**
   - **Decision:** Primary button - encourages users to start sessions.

3. **Should empty state show helpful text?**
   - **Decision:** Yes, show "No sessions yet. Create one to start development."
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/project-sessions-link/design.md

````
Wrote file successfully.

╰─────────╯

+## Context
+
+The MIMO platform currently has a ProjectDetailPage that shows project metadata (name, description, repo URL, type, owner, created date) but provides no visibility into sessions. Users must manually navigate to `/projects/:projectId/sessions` to view or create sessions, which is not discoverable.

+The session management functionality already exists:

+→ **Future:** Could add WebSocket for live status, but not needed for MVP

+3. No rollback needed - additive change

  "description": "Detailed specifications for the change",
  "instruction": "Create specification files that define WHAT the system should do.\n\nCreate one spec file per capability listed in the proposal's Capabilities section.\n- New capabilities: use the exact kebab-case name from the proposal (specs/<capability>/spec.md).\n- Modified capabilities: use the existing spec folder name from openspec/specs/<capability>/ when creating the delta spec at specs/<capability>/spec.md.\n\nDelta operations (use ## headers):\n- **ADDED Requirements**: New capabilities\n- **MODIFIED Requirements**: Changed behavior - MUST include full updated content\n- **REMOVED Requirements**: Deprecated features - MUST include **Reason** and **Migration**\n- **RENAMED Requirements**: Name changes only - use FROM:/TO: format\n\nFormat requirements:\n- Each requirement: `### Requirement: <name>` followed by description\n- Use SHALL/MUST for normative requirements (avoid should/may)\n- Each scenario: `#### Scenario: <name>` with WHEN/THEN format\n- **CRITICAL**: Scenarios MUST use exactly 4 hashtags (`####`). Using 3 hashtags or bullets will fail silently.\n- Every requirement MUST have at least one scenario.\n\nMODIFIED requirements workflow:\n1. Locate the existing requirement in openspec/specs/<capability>/spec.md\n2. Copy the ENTIRE requirement block (from `### Requirement:` through all scenarios)\n3. Paste under `## MODIFIED Requirements` and edit to reflect new behavior\n4. Ensure header text matches exactly (whitespace-insensitive)\n\nCommon pitfall: Using MODIFIED with partial content loses detail at archive time.\nIf adding new concerns without changing existing behavior, use ADDED instead.\n\nExample:\n```\n## ADDED Requirements\n\n### Requirement: User can export data\nThe system SHALL allow users to export their data in CSV format.\n\n#### Scenario: Successful export\n- **WHEN** user clicks \"Export\" button\n- **THEN** system downloads a CSV file with all user data\n\n## REMOVED Requirements\n\n### Requirement: Legacy export\n**Reason**: Replaced by new export system\n**Migration**: Use new export endpoint at /api/v2/export\n```\n\nSpecs should be testable - each scenario is a potential test case.\n",
  "template": "## ADDED Requirements\n\n### Requirement: <!-- requirement name -->\n<!-- requirement text -->\n\n#### Scenario: <!-- scenario name -->\n- **WHEN** <!-- condition -->\n- **THEN** <!-- expected outcome -->\n",
  "dependencies": [
    {
      "id": "proposal",
      "done": true,

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/project-sessions-link/specs/project-session-overview/spec.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:10:01
**Parameters:**
content: ## ADDED Requirements

### Requirement: Project detail page displays sessions
The system SHALL display a list of all sessions for a project on the project detail page.

#### Scenario: View sessions for a project with sessions
- **WHEN** user navigates to project detail page
- **AND** project has 3 existing sessions
- **THEN** system displays all 3 sessions in a Sessions section
- **AND** each session shows session name
- **AND** each session shows creation date
- **AND** each session name is a clickable link to session detail

#### Scenario: View sessions for a project with no sessions
- **WHEN** user navigates to project detail page
- **AND** project has 0 sessions
- **THEN** system displays "No sessions yet. Create one to start development."
- **AND** system displays "New Session" button

#### Scenario: Session list ordered by recency
- **WHEN** user views session list on project page
- **THEN** sessions are displayed in descending order by creation date
- **AND** most recent session appears first

### Requirement: Project detail page provides session creation
The system SHALL provide a "New Session" button on the project detail page to create new sessions.

#### Scenario: Create new session from project page
- **WHEN** user clicks "New Session" button
- **THEN** system navigates to `/projects/{projectId}/sessions/new`
- **AND** session creation form is displayed

#### Scenario: New Session button always visible
- **WHEN** user views project detail page
- **THEN** "New Session" button is visible regardless of existing session count
- **AND** button is styled as primary action (filled background)

### Requirement: Session links navigate to session detail
The system SHALL allow users to navigate to session detail from the project page.

#### Scenario: Click session to view details
- **WHEN** user clicks on session name in the list
- **THEN** system navigates to `/projects/{projectId}/sessions/{sessionId}`
- **AND** session detail page is displayed with full session information

#### Scenario: Session detail maintains project context
- **WHEN** user navigates to session detail from project page
- **AND** clicks "Back" in browser
- **THEN** system returns to project detail page
- **AND** session list is preserved
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/project-sessions-link/specs/project-session-overview/spec.md

```

<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/project-sessions-link/proposal.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## Why
2: 
3: Users cannot view or create sessions from the project detail page. When viewing a project, users see project metadata but have no visibility into existing sessions or a way to start new development sessions. The project-management spec states that selecting a project should "display project's sessions," but this requirement is not implemented.
4: 
5: ## What Changes
6: 
7: - **NEW**: Sessions section on ProjectDetailPage showing list of existing sessions
8: - **NEW**: "New Session" button linking to `/projects/:id/sessions/new`
9: - **NEW**: Session list with session name, status, and link to session detail
10: - **MODIFIED**: ProjectDetailPage to include sessions UI alongside project metadata
11: 
12: ## Capabilities
13: 
14: ### New Capabilities
15: 
16: - `project-session-overview`: Users can view all sessions for a project and create new sessions directly from the project detail page
17: 
18: ### Modified Capabilities
19: 
20: - `project-management`: Add requirement for displaying sessions on project detail page (already partially specified but not implemented)
21: 
22: ## Impact

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/project-sessions-link/design.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:11:26
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/project-sessions-link/design.md

````
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/project-sessions-link/design.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## Context
2: 
3: The MIMO platform currently has a ProjectDetailPage that shows project metadata (name, description, repo URL, type, owner, created date) but provides no visibility into sessions. Users must manually navigate to `/projects/:projectId/sessions` to view or create sessions, which is not discoverable.
4: 
5: The session management functionality already exists:
6: - `GET /projects/:projectId/sessions` - Lists sessions for a project
7: - `GET /projects/:projectId/sessions/new` - Shows session creation form
8: - `POST /projects/:projectId/sessions` - Creates a new session
9: - SessionRepository has `listByProject(projectId)` method
10: 
11: ## Goals / Non-Goals
12: 
13: **Goals:**
14: - Display existing sessions on the ProjectDetailPage
15: - Provide a clear "New Session" button to start development
16: - Show session name, ID, and status for each session
17: - Link sessions to their detail pages
18: 
19: **Non-Goals:**
20: - Session creation directly on project page (keep separate form)
21: - Session filtering or search (future enhancement)
22: - Session statistics or metrics (future enhancement)
23: - Deleting sessions from project page (keep on session detail)
24: 
25: ## Decisions
26: 
27: ### 1. Session Section Placement
28: 
29: **Decision:** Add a "Sessions" section below project details and above the actions section.
30: 
31: **Rationale:**
32: - Sessions are the primary workflow in MIMO - users create sessions to work on code
33: - Placing after project details provides context before actions
34: - Natural reading flow: project info → sessions → actions
35: 
36: **Alternatives considered:**
37: - Tab-based UI: Over-engineered for current needs, can add later if needed
38: - Side-by-side layout: Doesn't work well on mobile/tablet, more complex
39: - Separate sessions page: Existing, but lack of discoverability is the problem
40: 
41: ### 2. Session List Display
42: 
43: **Decision:** Show session name, creation date, and link to session detail.
44: 
45: **Rationale:**
46: - Minimal but useful information
47: - Consistent with existing project list pattern
48: - Clicking session name navigates to session detail page
49: 
50: **Implementation:**
51: ```tsx
52: <div class="sessions-section">
53:   <h2>Sessions</h2>
54:   {sessions.length === 0 ? (
55:     <p>No sessions yet. Create one to start development.</p>
56:   ) : (
57:     <ul>
58:       {sessions.map(session => (
59:         <li>
60:           <a href={`/projects/${projectId}/sessions/${session.id}`}>{session.name}</a>
61:           <span>{new Date(session.createdAt).toLocaleDateString()}</span>
62:         </li>
63:       ))}
64:     </ul>
65:   )}
66:   <a href={`/projects/${projectId}/sessions/new`} class="btn">New Session</a>
67: </div>
68: ```
69: 
70: ### 3. Data Fetching
71: 
72: **Decision:** Fetch sessions server-side in the existing `/projects/:id` route handler.
73: 
74: **Rationale:**
75: - Consistent with existing patterns (project list fetches projects)
76: - No additional API calls from client
77: - Simple to implement - just add one repository call
78: 
79: **Implementation:**
80: ```typescript
81: // In routes.tsx, GET /projects/:id
82: const sessions = await sessionRepository.listByProject(project.id);
83: return c.html(<ProjectDetailPage project={project} sessions={sessions} />);
84: ```
85: 
86: ## Risks / Trade-offs
87: 
88: **Risk:** Many sessions could make page long
89: → **Mitigation:** Show most recent 5 sessions with "View All" link (future), or add pagination
90: 
91: **Risk:** Stale session data if sessions change frequently
92: → **Mitigation:** Not a concern - page loads fresh on each request, no caching
93: 
94: **Risk:** Performance impact from additional database call
95: → **Mitigation:** Session list is small (typically <10), minimal overhead
96: 
97: **Trade-off:** No real-time session status updates
98: → **Future:** Could add WebSocket for live status, but not needed for MVP
99: 
100: ## Migration Plan
101: 
102: 1. Deploy code changes (no data migration needed)
103: 2. Users immediately see sessions on project detail page
104: 3. No rollback needed - additive change
105: 
106: ## Open Questions
107: 
108: 1. **Should we show active agents count per session?**
109:    - **Decision:** No, keep minimal. Can add later if needed.
110: 
111: 2. **Should "New Session" be primary (filled) or secondary (outline) button?**
112:    - **Decision:** Primary button - encourages users to start sessions.
113: 
114: 3. **Should empty state show helpful text?**
115:    - **Decision:** Yes, show "No sessions yet. Create one to start development."

(End of file - total 115 lines)
</content>
````

53:   async create(input: CreateSessionInput): Promise<Session> {
54:     const id = this.generateId();
55:     const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(input.projectId, id);
56:     const worktreePath = this.getWorktreePath(input.projectId, id);
57:     
58:     // Create session directory
59:     if (!existsSync(sessionPath)) {
60:       mkdirSync(sessionPath, { recursive: true });
61:     }
62: 
63:     // Create worktree directory
64:     if (!existsSync(worktreePath)) {
65:       mkdirSync(worktreePath, { recursive: true });
66:     }
67: 
68:     const now = new Date().toISOString();
69:     const sessionData: SessionData = {
70:       id,
71:       name: input.name,
72:       projectId: input.projectId,
73:       owner: input.owner,
74:       worktreePath,
75:       status: "active",
76:       createdAt: now,
77:       updatedAt: now,
78:     };
79: 
80:     writeFileSync(
81:       this.getSessionFilePath(input.projectId, id),
82:       dump(sessionData),
83:       "utf-8"
84:     );

87:       ...sessionData,

113:               updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
114:             };
115:           }

117:       }

143:   }
144: 
145:   try {

147:       name,
148:       repoUrl,

157:   }

newString: import type { FC } from "hono/jsx";
import { Layout } from "./Layout.js";

interface Project {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  repoUrl: string;
  repoType: "git" | "fossil";
  owner: string;
  createdAt: Date;
  description?: string;
}

interface Session {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  projectId: string;
  owner: string;
  worktreePath: string;
  status: "active" | "paused" | "closed";
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

interface ProjectDetailProps {
  project: Project;
  sessions: Session[];
}

export const ProjectDetailPage: FC<ProjectDetailProps> = ({ project, sessions }) => {
  const sortedSessions = sessions.sort((a, b) => 
    new Date(b.createdAt).getTime() - new Date(a.createdAt).getTime()
  );

  return (
    <Layout title={project.name}>
      <div class="container" style="max-width: 800px;">
        <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; margin-bottom: 20px;">
          <h1>{project.name}</h1>
          <div style="display: flex; gap: 10px;">
            <a href={`/projects/${project.id}/edit`} class="btn">Edit</a>
            <a href="/projects" class="btn-secondary">Back to Projects</a>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div class="project-details">
          {project.description && (
            <div class="detail-row">
              <label>Description:</label>
              <div style="line-height: 1.6;">{project.description}</div>
            </div>
          )}
          <div class="detail-row">
            <label>Repository URL:</label>
            <div>{project.repoUrl}</div>
          </div>
          <div class="detail-row">
            <label>Repository Type:</label>
            <div>{project.repoType}</div>
          </div>
          <div class="detail-row">
            <label>Owner:</label>
            <div>{project.owner}</div>
          </div>
          <div class="detail-row">
            <label>Created:</label>
            <div>{new Date(project.createdAt).toLocaleString()}</div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div style="margin-top: 30px;">
          <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; margin-bottom: 15px;">
            <h2 style="margin: 0;">Sessions</h2>
            <a href={`/projects/${project.id}/sessions/new`} class="btn">New Session</a>
          </div>
          
          {sortedSessions.length === 0 ? (
            <div class="empty-state">
              <p>No sessions yet. Create one to start development.</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div class="session-list">
              {sortedSessions.map((session) => (
                <div key={session.id} class="session-card">
                  <div class="session-header">
                    <a href={`/projects/${project.id}/sessions/${session.id}`} class="session-name">
                      {session.name}
                    </a>
                    <span class={`session-status ${session.status}`}>{session.status}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div class="session-meta">
                    <span>Created: {new Date(session.createdAt).toLocaleDateString()}</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        <div class="actions" style="margin-top: 30px;">
          <h2>Actions</h2>
          <form method="POST" action={`/projects/${project.id}/delete`} style="margin-top: 15px;">
            <button type="submit" class="btn-danger">Delete Project</button>
          </form>
        </div>
      </div>
    </Layout>
  );
};

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/test/project-sessions-link.test.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-04 00:13:21
**Parameters:**
content: import { describe, it, expect, beforeEach } from "bun:test";
import { Hono } from "hono";
import { tmpdir } from "os";
import { join } from "path";
import { rmSync } from "fs";
import bcrypt from "bcrypt";

let app: any;
let projectRepository: any;
let sessionRepository: any;
let userRepository: any;

describe("Project Sessions Link Integration Tests", () => {
  const testHome = join(tmpdir(), `mimo-project-sessions-test-${Date.now()}`);

  beforeEach(async () => {
    process.env.MIMO_HOME = testHome;
    process.env.JWT_SECRET = "test-secret-key-for-testing";

    try {
      rmSync(testHome, { recursive: true, force: true });
    } catch {}

    const pathsModule = await import("../src/config/paths.ts");
    pathsModule.ensureMimoHome();

    const userModule = await import("../src/auth/user.ts");
    userRepository = userModule.userRepository;

    const projectModule = await import("../src/projects/repository.ts");
    projectRepository = projectModule.projectRepository;

    const sessionModule = await import("../src/sessions/repository.ts");
    sessionRepository = sessionModule.sessionRepository;

    app = new Hono();
    
    const authModule = await import("../src/auth/routes.tsx");
    app.route("/auth", authModule.default);

    const protectedModule = await import("../src/protected/routes.tsx");
    app.route("/", protectedModule.default);

    const projectsModule = await import("../src/projects/routes.tsx");
    app.route("/projects", projectsModule.default);
  });

  describe("Project Detail Page with Sessions", () => {
    it("should show sessions list on project detail page", async () => {
      await userRepository.create("testuser", await bcrypt.hash("testpass", 10));
      const { generateToken } = await import("../src/auth/jwt.ts");
      const token = await generateToken("testuser");

      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "Test Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
      });

      await sessionRepository.create({
        name: "Feature Implementation",
        projectId: project.id,
        owner: "testuser",
        worktreePath: "",
      });

      await sessionRepository.create({
        name: "Bug Fix",
        projectId: project.id,
        owner: "testuser",
        worktreePath: "",
      });

      const res = await app.request(`/projects/${project.id}`, {
        headers: { Cookie: `token=${token}` },
      });

      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
      const html = await res.text();
      expect(html).toContain("Sessions");
      expect(html).toContain("Feature Implementation");
      expect(html).toContain("Bug Fix");
    });

    it("should show empty state when no sessions exist", async () => {
      await userRepository.create("testuser", await bcrypt.hash("testpass", 10));
      const { generateToken } = await import("../src/auth/jwt.ts");
      const token = await generateToken("testuser");

      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "Empty Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
      });

      const res = await app.request(`/projects/${project.id}`, {
        headers: { Cookie: `token=${token}` },
      });

      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
      const html = await res.text();
      expect(html).toContain("No sessions yet. Create one to start development.");
    });

    it("should show New Session button", async () => {
      await userRepository.create("testuser", await bcrypt.hash("testpass", 10));
      const { generateToken } = await import("../src/auth/jwt.ts");
      const token = await generateToken("testuser");

      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "Test Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
      });

      const res = await app.request(`/projects/${project.id}`, {
        headers: { Cookie: `token=${token}` },
      });

      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
      const html = await res.text();
      expect(html).toContain("New Session");
      expect(html).toContain(`/projects/${project.id}/sessions/new`);
    });

    it("should show session links to session detail", async () => {
      await userRepository.create("testuser", await bcrypt.hash("testpass", 10));
      const { generateToken } = await import("../src/auth/jwt.ts");
      const token = await generateToken("testuser");

      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "Test Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
      });

      const session = await sessionRepository.create({
        name: "Test Session",
        projectId: project.id,
        owner: "testuser",
        worktreePath: "",
      });

      const res = await app.request(`/projects/${project.id}`, {
        headers: { Cookie: `token=${token}` },
      });

      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
      const html = await res.text();
      expect(html).toContain(`/projects/${project.id}/sessions/${session.id}`);
    });

    it("should order sessions by creation date (most recent first)", async () => {
      await userRepository.create("testuser", await bcrypt.hash("testpass", 10));
      const { generateToken } = await import("../src/auth/jwt.ts");
      const token = await generateToken("testuser");

      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "Test Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
      });

      const session1 = await sessionRepository.create({
        name: "First Session",
        projectId: project.id,
        owner: "testuser",
        worktreePath: "",
      });

      // Small delay to ensure different timestamps
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 10));

      const session2 = await sessionRepository.create({
        name: "Second Session",
        projectId: project.id,
        owner: "testuser",
        worktreePath: "",
      });

      const res = await app.request(`/projects/${project.id}`, {
        headers: { Cookie: `token=${token}` },
      });

      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
      const html = await res.text();
      
      // Second session should appear before first in the HTML
      const secondIndex = html.indexOf("Second Session");
      const firstIndex = html.indexOf("First Session");
      expect(secondIndex).toBeLessThan(firstIndex);
    });
  });
});
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/test/project-sessions-link.test.ts

+import { describe, it, expect, beforeEach } from "bun:test";
+import { Hono } from "hono";
+import { tmpdir } from "os";
+import { join } from "path";
+import { rmSync } from "fs";
+import bcrypt from "bcrypt";
+
+let app: any;
+let projectRepository: any;
+let sessionRepository: any;
+let userRepository: any;
+
+describe("Project Sessions Link Integration Tests", () => {
+  const testHome = join(tmpdir(), `mimo-project-sessions-test-${Date.now()}`);
+
+  beforeEach(async () => {
+    process.env.MIMO_HOME = testHome;
+    process.env.JWT_SECRET = "test-secret-key-for-testing";
+
+    try {
+      rmSync(testHome, { recursive: true, force: true });
+    } catch {}
+
+    const pathsModule = await import("../src/config/paths.ts");
+    pathsModule.ensureMimoHome();
+
+    const userModule = await import("../src/auth/user.ts");
+    userRepository = userModule.userRepository;
+
+    const projectModule = await import("../src/projects/repository.ts");
+    projectRepository = projectModule.projectRepository;
+
+    const sessionModule = await import("../src/sessions/repository.ts");
+    sessionRepository = sessionModule.sessionRepository;
+
+    app = new Hono();
+    
+    const authModule = await import("../src/auth/routes.tsx");
+    app.route("/auth", authModule.default);
+
+    const protectedModule = await import("../src/protected/routes.tsx");
+    app.route("/", protectedModule.default);
+
+    const projectsModule = await import("../src/projects/routes.tsx");
+    app.route("/projects", projectsModule.default);
+  });
+
+  describe("Project Detail Page with Sessions", () => {
+    it("should show sessions list on project detail page", async () => {
+      await userRepository.create("testuser", await bcrypt.hash("testpass", 10));
+      const { generateToken } = await import("../src/auth/jwt.ts");
+      const token = await generateToken("testuser");
+
+      const project = await projectRepository.create({
+        name: "Test Project",
+        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
+        repoType: "git",
+        owner: "testuser",
+      });
+
+      await sessionRepository.create({
+        name: "Feature Implementation",
+        projectId: project.id,
+        owner: "testuser",
+        worktreePath: "",
+      });
+
+      await sessionRepository.create({
+        name: "Bug Fix",
+        projectId: project.id,
+        owner: "testuser",
+        worktreePath: "",
+      });
+
+      const res = await app.request(`/projects/${project.id}`, {
+        headers: { Cookie: `token=${token}` },
+      });
+
+      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
+      const html = await res.text();
+      expect(html).toContain("Sessions");
+      expect(html).toContain("Feature Implementation");
+      expect(html).toContain("Bug Fix");
+    });
+
+    it("should show empty state when no sessions exist", async () => {
+      await userRepository.create("testuser", await bcrypt.hash("testpass", 10));
+      const { generateToken } = await import("../src/auth/jwt.ts");
+      const token = await generateToken("testuser");
+
+      const project = await projectRepository.create({
+        name: "Empty Project",
+        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
+        repoType: "git",
+        owner: "testuser",
+      });
+
+      const res = await app.request(`/projects/${project.id}`, {
+        headers: { Cookie: `token=${token}` },
+      });
+
+      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
+      const html = await res.text();
+      expect(html).toContain("No sessions yet. Create one to start development.");
+    });
+
+    it("should show New Session button", async () => {
+      await userRepository.create("testuser", await bcrypt.hash("testpass", 10));
+      const { generateToken } = await import("../src/auth/jwt.ts");
+      const token = await generateToken("testuser");
+
+      const project = await projectRepository.create({
+        name: "Test Project",
+        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
+        repoType: "git",

+      });

+      const res = await app.request(`/projects/${project.id}`, {
